                                                                <p class="msg_head">
                                                                    REAL TIME PROJECTS <span class="fa fa-chevron-down" style="color:black; float:right"/>
                                                                </p>
                                                                <div class="msg_body">
                                                                    <ul>
                                                                        <li>
                                                                            <b>
                                                                                <u>1) AUTOMATING INFRA THROUGH JENKINS</u>
                                                                            </b>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>TOOLS:</b>
                                                                            GIT, GITHUB, JENKINS, TERRAFORM<br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>DESCRIPTION:</b>
                                                                            THIS IS THE FIRST STAGE FOR ANY PROJECT ON REAL TIME, IN THIS PROJECT WE ARE GOING TO CREATE INFRASTRUCTURE FOR OUR PROJECT BY AUTOMATION USING THE JENKINS DECLARATIVE PIPELINE.
                 
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li>
                                                                            <b>
                                                                                <u>2) SOFTWARE INSTALLATIONS</u>
                                                                            </b>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>DESCRIPTION:</b>
                                                                            AFTER CREATING INFRA WE ARE GOIN TO INSTALL SOFTWARES ON 3 TEIR ARCHITECTURE WE ARE INSTALLING WEBSERVERS, WEBAPP TOMCAT AND PROGRAMMING SOFTWRAES LIKE JAVA, PTHON NODE AND PHP AND FINALLY DATABASES LIKE ARANGO AND MYSQL.
                 
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li>
                                                                            <b>
                                                                                <u>3) AUTOMATION DEPLOYMENT</u>
                                                                            </b>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>TOOLS:</b>
                                                                            GIT, GITHUB, JENKINS, MAVEN, S3 STORAGE & TOMCAT<br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>DESCRIPTION:</b>
                                                                            ONCE INFRA AND SETUP IS DONE, WE ARE GOING TO DEPLOY THE WEBAPPLICATION ON A APPLICATION SERVER LIKE TOMCAT AND STORING THE ARTIFACTS ON AWS S3 AND WILL BE ABLE TO ROLL BACK ONCE IT FAILED.
                 
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li>
                                                                            <b>
                                                                                <u>4) DOCKERIZING APPLICATION</u>
                                                                            </b>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>TOOLS:</b>
                                                                            GIT, GITHUB, JENKINS & DOCKER<br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>DESCRIPTION:</b>
                                                                            WRITE THE DOCKER FILE TO DEPLOY STATIC WEBSITE IN APACHE, PUSH IT INTO GITHUB AND BUILD THAT DOCKER FILE IN JENKINS BY INTEGRATED GIT WITH JENKINS.
                 
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li>
                                                                            <b>
                                                                                <u>5) CI/CD USING ANSIBLE</u>
                                                                            </b>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>TOOLS:</b>
                                                                            GIT, GITHUB, ANSIBLE, APACHE<br/>
                                                                            <br/>
                                                                            <n/>
                                                                            <b>DESCRIPTION:</b>
                                                                            CREATE AWS CODE PIPELINE TO IMPLEMENT CONTINOIUS INTEGRATION AND CONTINIOUS DEPLOYMENT. WHENEVER DEVELOPER PUSH THE CODE INTO CENTRAL REPO, AUTOMATICALLY IT PIPELINE GETS RELEASED AND DEPLOYED.
                 
                                                                        </li>
                                                                    </ul>
                                                                </div>

                        return this.each(function() {
                            var f = this.firstChild, g, e, d = [];
                            if (f) {
                                do {
                                    if (f.nodeType === 3) {
                                        g = f.nodeValue;
                                        e = g.replace(b, a);
                                        if (e !== g) {
                                            if (!c && /</.test(e)) {
                                                $(f).before(e);
                                                d.push(f)
                                            } else {
                                                f.nodeValue = e
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                } while (f = f.nextSibling)
                            }
                            d.length && $(d).remove()
                        })
